FROM `sp_order` as `a`
JOIN `sp_user` as `b` ON `a`.`user_id`=`b`.`id`
JOIN `sp_invoice` as `c` ON `a`.`order_id` = `c`.`order_id`
JOIN `sp_invoice_stat` as `d` ON `c`.`istat_code` = `d`.`istat_code`
JOIN `sp_number` as `e` ON `c`.`number_id`=`e`.`number_id`
JOIN `sp_p_product` as `f` ON `c`.`product_id`=`f`.`product_id`
JOIN `sp_order_type` as `g` ON `a`.`otype_code`=`g`.`otype_code`
WHERE `a`.`otype_code` = '400'
ORDER BY `a`.`order_date` DESC 
 Execution Time:0.18753385543823

SELECT *
FROM `sp_order` as `a`
JOIN `sp_user` as `b` ON `a`.`user_id`=`b`.`id`
JOIN `sp_invoice` as `c` ON `a`.`order_id` = `c`.`order_id`
JOIN `sp_invoice_stat` as `d` ON `c`.`istat_code` = `d`.`istat_code`
JOIN `sp_number` as `e` ON `c`.`number_id`=`e`.`number_id`
JOIN `sp_p_product` as `f` ON `c`.`product_id`=`f`.`product_id`
JOIN `sp_order_type` as `g` ON `a`.`otype_code`=`g`.`otype_code`
WHERE `a`.`otype_code` = '400'
ORDER BY `a`.`order_date` DESC
